# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've successfully compiled a comprehensive analysis of all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the GroupCoordinator. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

**Core Implementation Files:**
1. **GroupCoordinator Interface** - Defines the coordination API
2. **GroupCoordinatorService** - Primary implementation of GroupCoordinator
3. **GroupCoordinatorShard** - Shard-level coordinator handling individual requests
4. **GroupMetadataManager** - Core state machine managing all group operations

**State Machine Implementation:**
- **ClassicGroupState.java** - Defines the five group states:
  - EMPTY
  - PREPARING_REBALANCE
  - COMPLETING_REBALANCE
  - STABLE
  - DEAD

**Group Type Implementations:**
- **Classic Groups** (ClassicGroup, ClassicGroupMember)
- **Modern Consumer Groups** (ConsumerGroup, ConsumerGroupMember)
- **Share Groups** (ShareGroup, ShareGroupMember)
- **Streams Groups** (StreamsGroup, StreamsGroupMember)

**Request Handlers:**
- JoinGroup and SyncGroup handlers routed through KafkaApis.scala
- Heartbeat request handlers for all group types (classic, consumer, share, streams)
- Heartbeat expiry detection through rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()

\"text\": \"The Apache Kafka GroupCoordinator implementation is spread across multiple files in the group-coordinator module and related modules. The core architecture includes:\\n\\n**Main GroupCoordinator Interface and Implementation:**\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for group coordination operations. The primary implementation is GroupCoordinatorService (GroupCoordinatorService.java), which implements the GroupCoordinator interface and delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard for request handling. The GroupCoordinatorShard class (GroupCoordinatorShard.java) is the actual shard-level coordinator that handles individual requests and delegates to GroupMetadataManager for business logic.\\n\\n**Group Metadata State Machine:**\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (GroupMetadataManager.java) is the core state machine manager that handles all group metadata operations. It manages three types of consumer groups:\\n\\n1. **Classic Groups** - Implement the original Kafka consumer group protocol:\\n   - ClassicGroup.java: Main group class managing classic groups with states (EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, DEAD)\\n   - ClassicGroupState.java: Enum defining the five group states with valid state transitions\\n   - ClassicGroupMember.java: Represents a member in a classic group\\n\\n2. **Modern Consumer Groups** - Implement the new consumer group protocol:\\n   - ConsumerGroup.java: Modern consumer group implementation\\n   - ConsumerGroupMember.java: Modern consumer group member\\n   - CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java: Builds current assignment for modern groups\\n\\n3. **Share Groups** - For shared consumption:\\n   - ShareGroup.java: Share group implementation\\n   - ShareGroupMember.java: Share group member\\n   - ShareGroupConfig.java: Share group configuration\\n   - ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java: Assignment builder for share groups\\n\\n4. **Streams Groups** - For Kafka Streams applications:\\n   - StreamsGroup.java: Streams group implementation\\n   - StreamsGroupMember.java: Streams group member\\n   - StreamsGroupHeartbeatResult.java: Heartbeat result wrapper\\n\\n**JoinGroup and SyncGroup Request Handlers:**\\nThe request handlers are implemented in multiple layers:\\n- KafkaApis.scala The core architecture includes:\\n\\n**Main GroupCoordinator Interface and Implementation:**\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for group coordination operations. The primary implementation is GroupCoordinatorService (GroupCoordinatorService.java), which implements the GroupCoordinator interface and delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard for request handling. The GroupCoordinatorShard class (GroupCoordinatorShard.java) is the actual shard-level coordinator that handles individual requests and delegates to GroupMetadataManager for business logic.\\n\\n**Group Metadata State Machine:**\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (GroupMetadataManager.java) is the core state machine manager that handles all group metadata operations. It manages three types of consumer groups:\\n\\n1. **Classic Groups** - Implement the original Kafka consumer group protocol:\\n   - ClassicGroup.java: Main group class managing classic groups with states (EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, DEAD)\\n   - ClassicGroupState.java: Enum defining the five group states with valid state transitions\\n   - ClassicGroupMember.java: Represents a member in a classic group\\n\\n2. **Modern Consumer Groups** - Implement the new consumer group protocol:\\n   - ConsumerGroup.java: Modern consumer group implementation\\n   - ConsumerGroupMember.java: Modern consumer group member\\n   - CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java: Builds current assignment for modern groups\\n\\n3. **Share Groups** - For shared consumption:\\n   - ShareGroup.java: Share group implementation\\n   - ShareGroupMember.java: Share group member\\n   - ShareGroupConfig.java: Share group configuration\\n   - ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java: Assignment builder for share groups\\n\\n4. **Streams Groups** - For Kafka Streams applications:\\n   - StreamsGroup.java: Streams group implementation\\n   - StreamsGroupMember.java: Streams group member\\n   - (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains handleJoinGroupRequest and handleSyncGroupRequest which route to the group coordinator\\n- GroupCoordinatorService.java implements the public joinGroup and syncGroup methods\\n- GroupCoordinatorShard.java has joinGroup and syncGroup request handlers\\n- GroupMetadataManager.java contains the main business logic:\\n  - classicGroupJoin: Handles classic group join requests\\n  - classicGroupSync: Handles classic group sync requests\\n  - consumerGroupJoin: Handles modern consumer group join\\n\\n**Heartbeat Expiry handleStreamsGroupHeartbeat in KafkaApis.scala: Routes streams group heartbeats\\n- classicGroupHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Main heartbeat handler for classic groups\\n-
